<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Item&nbsp;2.02.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>Disclosure of Results of Operations and Financial Condition. </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">On July&nbsp;25, 2019 we issued the press release attached as Exhibit 99.1. It is incorporated into this report by reference. The press release
describes the results of our operations for the quarter and fiscal year ended June&nbsp;30, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><B>Item&nbsp;8.01.</B></TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="justify"><B>Other Events. </B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="justify">On July&nbsp;25, 2019, we announced that our board of directors declared a quarterly cash dividend of US $0.39 per share, an increase of 5% compared to
the most recent quarterly dividend of $0.37 per share. The dividend will have a record date of August&nbsp;15, 2019, payable on September&nbsp;19, 2019. The dividend will be paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#146;s common stock trading on
the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of Chess Depositary Instruments trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency, based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1 ratio
between CDIs and NYSE shares. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</FONT> date will be August&nbsp;14, 2019 for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed has received a waiver from the ASX&#146;s settlement operating rules, which
will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from August&nbsp;14, 2019 through August&nbsp;15, 2019, inclusive.</P> <P STYLE="font-size:36pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:30pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:13pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>ResMed Inc. Announces Results for the Fourth Quarter of Fiscal Year 2019 </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">

<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#150;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt"><I>Year-over-year revenue grows 13%, gross margin improves 120 basis points,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> operating profit up 18%</I> </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL"><I>Note: A webcast of ResMed&#146;s conference call will be available at 4:30 p.m. ET today at
<FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>http://investor.resmed.com</U></FONT> </I></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">SAN DIEGO, July&nbsp;25, 2019 &#150; ResMed Inc. (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD),
a world-leading connected health company, today announced results for its quarter ended June&nbsp;30, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:22pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Fourth Quarter 2019 Highlights </B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Revenue increased 13% to $705.0&nbsp;million; up 15% on a constant currency basis </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Gross margin expanded 120&nbsp;bps to 59.3% </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$0.95 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:22pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Full Year 2019 Highlights </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

$3.64 </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#147;We finished fiscal year 2019 with double-digit revenue growth to $2.6&nbsp;billion and operating profit up 18% on a <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> basis. Recent mask launches have driven market share gains while continued adoption of our SaaS solutions is driving both revenue growth and a steady margin profile,&#148; said Mick Farrell, ResMed&#146;s
CEO. &#147;We delivered another quarter of operating leverage, which gives us flexibility as we execute on our long-term strategy to provide innovative products, software, and solutions to improve health outcomes, create efficiencies, and reduce
overall healthcare system costs. Our pipeline is solid; we are well-positioned as we enter fiscal year 2020 on a trajectory to improve 250&nbsp;million lives in
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> healthcare in 2025.&#148; </P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:14pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">In order to provide a framework for assessing how our underlying businesses performed excluding the effect of foreign
currency fluctuations, we provide certain financial information on a &#147;constant currency basis&#148;, which is in addition to the actual financial information presented. In order to calculate our constant currency information, we translate the
current period financial information using the foreign currency exchange rates that were in effect during the previous comparable period. However, constant currency measures should not be considered in isolation or as an alternative to U.S. dollar
measures that reflect current period exchange rates, or to other financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with U.S. GAAP. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:8pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(B)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">See the reconciliation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures in the table at the end of
the press release. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Discussion of Fourth Quarter Results </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Revenue in the U.S., Canada, and Latin America, excluding Software as a Service, grew by 11&nbsp;percent compared to the
prior year period, driven by strong sales across our mask and device product portfolios. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Revenue in combined Europe, Asia and other markets grew by 4&nbsp;percent on a constant currency basis compared to the same
period of the prior year. Mask sales were strong across these markets. As expected, device sales in France and Japan were impacted as customers completed their connected device upgrade programs. Device sales outside France and Japan grew well.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Software as a Service revenue increased by 111&nbsp;percent, compared to the prior year period, due to continued growth in
Brightree service offerings and incremental contribution from the acquisition of MatrixCare, which closed in the second quarter, and HEALTHCARE<I>first, </I>which closed in the first quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left"><FONT STYLE="font-family:Times New Roman">&#9679;</FONT></TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:10pt">Gross margin expanded by 120 basis points over the prior year period, primarily due to higher margin contribution from
MatrixCare, benefits from manufacturing and procurement efficiencies, partially offset by declines in average selling prices. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="margin-top:14pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Dividend program </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">The ResMed board of directors today declared a
quarterly cash dividend of $0.39 per share, an increase of 5% compared to the most recent quarterly dividend of $0.37 per share. The dividend will have a record date of August&nbsp;15, 2019, payable on September&nbsp;19, 2019. The dividend will be
paid in U.S. currency to holders of ResMed&#146;s common stock trading on the New York Stock Exchange. Holders of Chess Depositary Instruments trading on the Australian Securities Exchange will receive an equivalent amount in Australian currency,
based on the exchange rate on the record date, and reflecting the 10:1 ratio between CDIs and NYSE shares. The <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">ex-dividend</FONT> date will be August&nbsp;14, 2019 for common stockholders and for CDI holders. ResMed
has received a waiver from the ASX&#146;s settlement operating rules, which will allow ResMed to defer processing conversions between its common stock and CDI registers from August&nbsp;14, 2019 through August&nbsp;15, 2019, inclusive.</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>About ResMed </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL">At ResMed (NYSE: RMD, ASX: RMD) we pioneer innovative
solutions that treat and keep people out of the hospital, empowering them to live healthier, higher-quality lives. Our cloud-connected medical devices transform care for people with sleep apnea, COPD and other chronic diseases. Our comprehensive <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-hospital</FONT></FONT> software platforms support the professionals and caregivers who help people stay healthy in the home or care setting of their choice. By enabling better care,
we improve quality of life, reduce the impact of chronic disease and lower costs for consumers and healthcare systems in more than 120 countries.&nbsp;To learn more, visit <FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#0000ff"><U>ResMed.com</U></FONT><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> and follow @ResMed. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B><I>Safe harbor statement </I></B></P>

Act of 1995. These forward-looking statements &#150; including statements regarding ResMed&#146;s projections of future revenue or earnings, expenses, new product development, new product launches, new markets for its products, the integration of
acquisitions, litigation, and tax outlook &#150; are subject to risks and uncertainties, which could cause actual results to materially differ from those projected or implied in the forward-looking statements. Additional risks and uncertainties are
discussed in ResMed&#146;s periodic reports on file with the U.S. Securities&nbsp;&amp; Exchange Commission. ResMed does not undertake to update its forward-looking statements. </P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(A)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL; " ALIGN="left">ResMed adjusts for the impact of the amortization of acquired intangibles, deferred revenue fair value adjustment,
acquisition-related expenses, restructuring-related expenses, litigation settlement expenses, fair value impairment of investment, and the impact of U.S. tax reform on income tax expense, from their evaluation of ongoing operations, and believes
that investors benefit from adjusting these items to facilitate a more meaningful evaluation of current operating performance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:8pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:8pt; font-family:ARIAL">ResMed believes that <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> diluted earnings per share is an additional measure of performance that investors
can use to compare operating results between reporting periods. ResMed uses <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> information internally in planning, forecasting, and evaluating the results of operations in the current period and in
comparing it to past periods. ResMed believes this information provides investors better insight when evaluating ResMed&#146;s performance from core operations and provides consistent financial reporting. The use of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures is intended to supplement, and not to replace, the presentation of net income and other GAAP measures. Like all <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> measures, <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> earnings are subject to inherent limitations because they do not include all the expenses that must be included under GAAP. </P>
